#Written by hiddengearz
#Inspired by the original Allied Construction Project https://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=1368202826
#This reworked system allows you to have 5 of each project active per country.
#So you can have 5 CIC projects, 5 INF projects, 5 MIC projects etc in every country in the game
#There are 8 project types * 5 of each allowed per country = 40 investments possibile in one country * 210 countries the player can invest in = 8400 possibile investments for the player
#Now if the AI also does the same that's 210 * 8400 = 1,764,000 possibile investments possibile




# BUILDING CONSTRUCTION COSTS

@BUILD_COST_INFRASTRUCTURE = 2.5
@BUILD_COST_AIRBASE = 1.5
@BUILD_COST_ANTIAIR = 1.5
@BUILD_COST_RADAR = 1.5
@BUILD_COST_MILITARY_FACTORY = 6
@BUILD_COST_CIVILIAN_FACTORY = 6
@BUILD_COST_DOCKYARD = 6
@BUILD_COST_REFINERY = 1

#Used to calculate how long it will take to build the building - called in the scripted gui
AC_update_build_time = {

	ROOT = {
		###construction speed default is 100%

		set_variable = { AC_construction_speed = 1 }
		#AC_get_building_values_for_gui = yes

		#Adds production speed modifier from investor
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_buildings_factor }
		multiply_variable = { AC_construction_speed = AC_target_state_infra_speed }
		### construction speed penalty for investments, they're just 25% slower
		multiply_variable = { AC_construction_speed = 0.75 }
		### total factory output - KR: changed to balance value
		divide_variable = { AC_construction_speed = 20 }
		### days to build

		set_variable = { AC_construction_duration = AC_build_cost } #build cost set by AC_update_build_cost, which is called in scripted gui
		divide_variable = { AC_construction_duration = AC_construction_speed }
		round_variable = AC_construction_duration
		#If you have one of these internal factions investments are 25% faster
		#If you change this update the tooltip for these internal factions
		if = { limit = { or = { has_idea = industrial_conglomerates has_idea = chaebols } }
			multiply_variable = { AC_construction_duration = 0.75 }
		}
		round_variable = AC_construction_duration

	}
}

#Sets the investment/build cost, called only in the scripted gui before starting the project
AC_update_build_cost = {
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 1 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_INFRASTRUCTURE }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 2 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_AIRBASE }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 3 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_ANTIAIR }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 4 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_RADAR }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 5 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_MILITARY_FACTORY }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 6 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_CIVILIAN_FACTORY }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 7 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_DOCKYARD }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 8 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_REFINERY }
	}
	multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = AC_build_amount }

	PREV = {
		### get infrastructure level from target country
		set_variable = { ROOT.AC_target_state_infra_speed = infrastructure_level }
	}
	#if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected > 4 } }

		multiply_variable = { AC_target_state_infra_speed = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { AC_target_state_infra_speed = -1 }

		add_to_variable = { AC_target_state_infra_speed = 1.5 }


	# }
	multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = AC_target_state_infra_speed } #Infrastructure changes cost


	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = paralyzing_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.45 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = crippling_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.40 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = rampant_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.35 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = unrestrained_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = systematic_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = widespread_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = medium_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = modest_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = slight_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = negligible_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}


	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_12 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 3.7 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_11 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 3.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_10 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_9 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_8 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.22 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_7 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_6 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.8 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_5 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.63 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_4 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.46 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_3 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_2 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_1 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}
	round_variable = AC_build_cost
}

#starts the project, called in scripted gui
#This effect is triggered when a country invests in another country.
#The default scope is state you're making your investment in, Root is the country initiating the investment (the investor),
#within ROOT scope PREV is the previous scope (so the state your making the investment in) and controller is the country that controls that state.
AC_start_project = {
	#AC_update_build_time = yes
	ROOT = {
		#Sets construction duration variable that was created in AC_update_build_time for the investor onto the country being invested in
		#Needed so the invest can see how long until the investors construction is complete
		PREV = { CONTROLLER = { set_variable = { AC_target_construction_duration = FROM.FROM.AC_construction_duration } } }

		#Update money
		subtract_from_variable = { treasury = AC_build_cost }
		add_to_variable = { int_investments = AC_build_cost }
		calculate_int_investments_rate = yes

		PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = Investment_pause_@ROOT value = 1 } } #You can only invest once in this state once a day

		### active project building type
		#These state flags set 1)How many of said building your making 2) If you have 1 of 5 allowed projects per coutry
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = { CONTROLLER = { not = { any_owned_state = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT } } } }
				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 2 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 3 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 4 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 5 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 6 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = { CONTROLLER = { not = { any_owned_state = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT } } } }
				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 2 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 3 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 4 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 5 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 6 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state2_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_CIC_target_state1_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = { CONTROLLER = { not = { any_owned_state = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT } } } }
				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 2 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 3 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 4 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 5 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 6 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state3_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = { CONTROLLER = { not = { any_owned_state = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT } } } }
				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 2 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 3 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 4 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 5 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 6 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state4_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = { CONTROLLER = { not = { any_owned_state = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT } } } }
				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 2 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 3 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 4 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 4 } }

				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 5 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 5 } }

					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}
			}


		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = { CONTROLLER = { not = { any_owned_state = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT } } } }
				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 2 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 2 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 3 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 4 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 5 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 6 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state1_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}

			else_if = {

				}
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 1 } }

					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state2_@ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 6 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state2_@ROOT value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 7 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_AB_target_state2_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }

					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 8 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 8 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 9 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 9 } }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_build_amount = 10 } }
					PREV = { set_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 10 } }
				}
			}


		}

		### send permission request to target
		#this state every 1 days
		PREV = {
			save_event_target_as = AC_state_event_target
			CONTROLLER = { country_event = AC_event.1 }
			#state_event = { id = AC_event.1 trigger_for = controller }
		}
	}
}

#I don't think this is used, leftover from allied construction project will check later
AC_get_building_values_for_gui = {
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 1 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_INFRASTRUCTURE }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_infrastructure_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 2 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_AIRBASE }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_air_base_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 3 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_ANTIAIR }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_anti_air_building_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 4 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_RADAR }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_radar_station_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 5 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_MILITARY_FACTORY }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_arms_factory_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 6 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_CIVILIAN_FACTORY }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_industrial_complex_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 7 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_DOCKYARD }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_dockyard_factor }
	}

	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 8 } }

		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_REFINERY }
		add_to_variable = { AC_construction_speed = modifier@production_speed_synthetic_refinery_factor }
	}
}

###Only used in the scripted gui when the investor decides to cancel the project via the scripted gui.

		}

			limit = {

			}
			PREV = { clr_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = AC_construction_INF_decision1 }

#######################################################################################################################
###All of the AC_add_XXX_building effects are used in decissions to add the building to the correct lcoation and etc
###All of the AC_add_XXX_building2 effects are used in the decission seen by the country being invested in to show them
###what will happen when the investment is finished, they're basically just tooltips
#######################################################################################################################
AC_add_INF_building = {

	if = {
		limit = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 1 }
			}
			add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 1 instant_build = yes }
			CONTROLLER = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = AC_construction_opinion } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 2 }
			}
			add_building_construction = { type = infrastructure level = 2 instant_build = yes }
			CONTROLLER = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = AC_construction_opinion2 } }
		}

		}
	}
}


#Should be identical to AC_update_build_cost (except for scopes) as that sets the original cost, this is a copy but with changed scopes
#and returns money instead of removing it
#Used in AC_Return_money_XXX effect
#this is used when the investor cancels the investment. Default scope is the investor, PREV is the state they invested in,
#if you use CONTROLLER within the PREV scope that would be the country that he invested in.
AC_Calculate_money_to_return = {
	log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: cost: [?Temp_AC_build_cost] ammount: [?Temp_AC_build_amount] "
	multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = Temp_AC_build_amount }
	log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: cost: [?Temp_AC_build_cost]"
	PREV = {
		### get infrastructure level from target country
		set_temp_variable = { ROOT.Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = infrastructure_level }
	}
	#if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected > 4 } }

		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = 0.05 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = -1 }

		add_to_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = 1.5 }

	# }
	multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed } #Infrastructure changes cost
	log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: cost: [?Temp_AC_build_cost]"

	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_12 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 3.7 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_11 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 3.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_10 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 2.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_9 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 2.5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_8 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 2.22 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_7 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 2.0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_6 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.8 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_5 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.63 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_4 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.46 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_3 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_2 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_1 } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}
	log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: cost: [?Temp_AC_build_cost]"

	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = paralyzing_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.45 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = crippling_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.40 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = rampant_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.35 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = unrestrained_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = systematic_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = widespread_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = medium_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = modest_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = slight_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = negligible_corruption } } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}
	log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: cost: [?Temp_AC_build_cost]"
	round_variable = Temp_AC_build_cost
	add_to_variable = { treasury = Temp_AC_build_cost }
	subtract_from_variable = { int_investments = Temp_AC_build_cost }
	calculate_int_investments_rate = yes

	set_variable = { Temp_AC_influence_cost = Temp_AC_build_cost }
	PREV = {
		CONTROLLER = {
			for_loop_effect = {
				end = influence_array^num
				value = v
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^v = ROOT }
					}

					log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: IA: [?influence_array^v] IAV: [?influence_array_val^v] TCost: [?ROOT.Temp_AC_influence_cost] "
					subtract_from_variable = { influence_array_val^v = ROOT.Temp_AC_influence_cost }
					log = "GEARZZZ [Root.GetName]: IA: [?influence_array^v] IAV: [?influence_array_val^v] TCost: [?ROOT.Temp_AC_influence_cost] "
				}
			}
			recalculate_influence = yes
		}
	}
	clear_variable  = Temp_AC_influence_cost
}

#Should be identical to AC_update_build_cost (except for scopes) as that sets the original cost, this is a copy but with changed scopes
#and returns money instead of removing it
##Used in AC_Return_money_XXX2 effect
#this is used when the investee cancels the investment. Default scope is the state that was invested in,
#if you use controller you'll be targeting the investee country. FROM is the investor.
AC_Calculate_money_to_return2 = {
	FROM = { multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = Temp_AC_build_amount } }
	### get infrastructure level from target country
	set_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = infrastructure_level }
	#if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected > 4 } }

		FROM = { multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = 0.05 } }
		FROM = { multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = -1 } }
		FROM = { add_to_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed = 1.5 } }
	# }
	FROM = { multiply_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = Temp_AC_target_state_infra_speed } } #Infrastructure changes cost
	if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_12 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 3.7 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_11 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 3.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_10 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 2.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_9 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 2.5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_8 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 2.22 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_7 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 2.0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_6 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 1.8 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_5 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 1.63 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_4 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 1.46 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_3 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_2 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_1 } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = paralyzing_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.45 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = crippling_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.40 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = rampant_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.35 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = unrestrained_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = systematic_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = widespread_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = medium_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = modest_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = slight_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = negligible_corruption } }
		multiply_temp_variable = { FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}
	FROM = {
		round_temp_variable = Temp_AC_build_cost
		add_to_variable = { treasury = Temp_AC_build_cost }
		subtract_from_variable = { int_investments = Temp_AC_build_cost }
		calculate_int_investments_rate = yes
	}

	set_variable = { Temp_AC_influence_cost = FROM.Temp_AC_build_cost }
	CONTROLLER = {
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = influence_array^num
			value = v
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { influence_array^v = FROM }
				}

				log = "GEARZZZ [FROM.GetName]: IA: [?influence_array^v] IAV: [?influence_array_val^v] TCost: [?FROM.Temp_AC_influence_cost] "
				subtract_from_variable = { influence_array_val^v = FROM.Temp_AC_influence_cost }
				log = "GEARZZZ [FROM.GetName]: IA: [?influence_array^v] IAV: [?influence_array_val^v] TCost: [?FROM.Temp_AC_influence_cost] "
			}
		}
		recalculate_influence = yes
	}

	clear_variable  = FROM.Temp_AC_influence_cost

}

#AC_Return_money_XXX checks for what flag is in state and how many buildings were invested, then calls
#AC_Calculate_money_to_return. Only used in AC_end_project
AC_Return_money_INF = {
	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT } }
		set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_INFRASTRUCTURE }
		if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 1 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 2 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 3 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 4 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 4 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 5 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 6 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 6 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 7 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 7 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 8 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 8 }

				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state1_@ROOT value = 9 } }

			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 3 }
		}

		}
		else_if = {

			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 9 }
		}

			}

		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { has_state_flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 1 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PREV = { has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_INF_target_state5_@ROOT value = 2 } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 2 }
		}

			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 4 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 4 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 5 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 5 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 6 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 6 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 7 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 7 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 8 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 8 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 9 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 9 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = { flag = AC_construction_REF_target_state5_@FROM value = 10 }
			}
			FROM = { set_temp_variable = { Temp_AC_build_amount = 10 } }
		}
	}
	AC_Calculate_money_to_return2 = yes
}

#Sets the investment/build cost, called only in the scripted gui before starting the project
AC_update_build_cost = {
	if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 1 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_INFRASTRUCTURE }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 2 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_AIRBASE }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 3 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_ANTIAIR }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 4 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_RADAR }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 5 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_MILITARY_FACTORY }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 6 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_CIVILIAN_FACTORY }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 7 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_DOCKYARD }
	}
	else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected = 8 } }
		set_variable = { AC_build_cost = @BUILD_COST_REFINERY }
	}
	multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = AC_build_amount }

	PREV = {
		### get infrastructure level from target country
		set_variable = { ROOT.AC_target_state_infra_speed = infrastructure_level }
	}
	#if = { limit = { check_variable = { AC_building_type_selected > 4 } }

		multiply_variable = { AC_target_state_infra_speed = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { AC_target_state_infra_speed = -1 }

		add_to_variable = { AC_target_state_infra_speed = 1.5 }


	# }
	multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = AC_target_state_infra_speed } #Infrastructure changes cost

	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = paralyzing_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.45 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = crippling_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.40 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = rampant_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.35 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = unrestrained_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = systematic_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = widespread_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = medium_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = modest_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = slight_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = negligible_corruption } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = mafia_foreign_investment } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 3.0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_12 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 3.7 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_11 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 3.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_10 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_9 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_8 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.22 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_7 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 2.0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_6 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.8 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_5 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.63 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_4 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.46 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_3 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_2 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { PREV = { CONTROLLER = { has_idea = gdp_1 } } }
		multiply_variable = { AC_build_cost = 1 }
	}

	round_variable = AC_build_cost


}

#Clears state flags if a state changes owners before an investment is don via AC_on_actions.txt on_state_control_changed
